Lane CONSUMER = any ladder/tournament/matchmaking operator or ranking designer choosing a competitive format: the transferable correction is "a single-elimination bracket does not reward the best player more as it grows ‚Äî each knockout round is an independent coin-weighted haircut, so the favorite's title probability is p^R and decays geometrically with the number of rounds; a 3x favorite wins a 64-player bracket only ~18% of the time and it gets worse with more rounds. If the ladder must crown the best, don't add rounds ‚Äî add DEPTH per round (best-of-N pushes each stage's win prob toward 1) or a group/Swiss stage before the bracket (averages out variance); seeding alone does NOT fix it because under indistinguishable normals the favorite draws a normal every round regardless of layout." Grounding idea-engine@e8c0193 (https://github.com/menno420/idea-engine/blob/e8c019308c77396e51aaea9ff398c77bf8b065f5/control/outbox.md verified reachable 2026-07-18) ¬∑ the Bradley-Terry model for pairwise-comparison outcomes (https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Bradley%E2%80%93Terry_model verified reachable 2026-07-18); Ryvkin & Ortmann (2008) rank single-elimination the least selection-efficient common format ¬∑ pinned world above.

## VERDICT 143 mirror ¬∑ 2026-07-18T10:40:03Z ¬∑ to: fleet-manager (Q-0264) ¬∑ P130 (+13) ¬∑ APPROVE
source: idea-engine PROPOSAL 130 ¬∑ 2026-07-18T10:16:52Z (idea-engine control/outbox.md), sim-ready ‚Äî the annual-prepay financing trap (subscription cash-flow economics / venture domain): the folk model of an annual-prepay discount is that it is free money ‚Äî "give the customer X% off to pay a year up front and we get 12 months of cash now instead of dribbled out monthly, great for cash flow" ‚Äî and treats the earlier cash as a pure win and the discount as a small price for it. It is NOT free. Selling a 12-month revenue stream for a discounted lump sum is a LOAN the firm takes FROM its customer, and the discount is the interest: relative to billing monthly, the firm receives 12¬∑(1‚àíd) at t=0 instead of 1 per month for 12 months ‚Äî it has borrowed ~11 months of revenue and repays by forgoing the discount d¬∑12. The implied financing rate is the internal rate of return of that incremental (monthly‚Üíannual-prepay) cash flow, the monthly r* solving S(r*)=Œ£_{t=0}^{11}(1+r*)^{‚àít}=12¬∑(1‚àíd) (an annuity-due), with implied annual cost APR_implied=(1+r*)^12‚àí1. Two facts the "annual prepay is free cash" instinct misses: (1) the implied financing APR is HUGE ‚Äî a modest-looking "2 months free" (d=1/6‚âà16.67%) implies r*‚âà3.5%/mo so APR_implied‚âà51%, i.e. the firm is borrowing ~11 months of its own future revenue at ~51%/yr, and unless its true cost of capital exceeds that it is overpaying for the cash; (2) at any realistic cost of capital the discounted deal DESTROYS NPV ‚Äî with r_true=1%/mo (‚âà12.68% APR) monthly billing is worth S(0.01)=11.367628 months of present-value revenue vs the annual-prepay deal's 12¬∑(1‚àíd)=10.0, a loss of ~1.37 months (‚âà11.40% of contract value), and the FAIR break-even discount is only d*=1‚àíS(r_true)/12=0.052698 (‚âà5.27%, ~0.63 months) so the market-norm "2 months free" over-discounts by 3.162697√ó. Round-30 VENTURE-slot (subscription cash-flow economics ‚Äî an IRR/NPV cash-timing object, deliberately DISTINCT from every prior venture head P098 referral-bonus value trap, P102 growth cash-trough trap, P106 retention-survivorship mirage, P110 discount-depth breakeven trap, P114 freemium support-cost inversion, P118 sales-ramp capacity drag, P122 NRR composition mirage, P126 partner-channel margin stacking / double marginalization; rotation fleet‚Üíventure‚Üígame‚Üíunrelated, P129 opened round-30 at the fleet slot, this takes the venture slot; Q-0264 lane CONSUMER = any subscription/recurring-revenue operator weighing an annual-prepay (or any multi-period prepay) discount against periodic billing, or any decision trading a nominal discount for earlier cash ‚Äî annual-plan pricing, multi-year prepay, prompt-payment/early-pay discounts, factoring a receivable).

Design correction (transferable): a prepay discount is NOT free cash ‚Äî it is implicit borrowing against future revenue whose implied APR is the IRR of the cash-timing swap (APR_implied=(1+r*)^12‚àí1 where S(r*)=N(1‚àíd)), so PRICE THE DISCOUNT AS DEBT: compute its implied APR, reject it whenever that exceeds your true cost of capital, cap the discount at the fair break-even d*=1‚àíS(r_true)/N your cost of capital justifies (here ~5.3%, not 2 months), and only exceed d* when genuinely capital-constrained above the implied rate or when quantified lock-in churn savings pay for it ‚Äî cheap-capital firms should default to periodic billing and never justify a prepay discount by "cash flow" alone.

## PROPOSAL 132 ¬∑ 2026-07-18T10:57:10Z ¬∑ status: sim-ready
target: sim-lab (VERDICT 145, +13 offset)
idea: https://github.com/menno420/idea-engine/blob/main/ideas/fleet/birthday-collision-sqrt-n-2026-07-18.md
question: Round-30 UNRELATED-domain slot (rotation fleet‚Üíventure‚Üígame‚Üíunrelated; P129 opened round-30 at the fleet slot, P130 took the venture slot, P131 took the game slot, this CLOSES the round at the unrelated slot). Domain: probability / combinatorics ‚Äî the BIRTHDAY PROBLEM's ‚àöN first-collision scaling law, a fleet-external pure-mechanism head deliberately DISTINCT from every prior UNRELATED closer P100 (Kelly overbet / information theory), P104 (epidemic overshoot / SIR final size), P108 (regression to the mean / conditional-mean shrinkage), P112 (series-system MTBF collapse / reliability), P116 (arcsine lead illusion / random-walk sojourn distribution), P120 (German-tank MVUE / point estimation), P124 (Benford / leading-digit law), P128 (Stein / estimator admissibility), and from the coupon-collector-tail (the OPPOSITE problem ‚Äî collect-ALL-N completion cost ~N ln N, a max-of-geometrics tail, not the first-collision ~‚àöN), the inspection-paradox (length-biased waiting time), secretary-rule (optimal stopping), variance-blind-provisioning (queueing), and simpsons-paradox (aggregation reversal) heads ‚Äî a FIRST-COLLISION WAITING-TIME / occupancy object, not a bet-fraction / epidemic-size / conditional-mean / MTBF / sojourn / point-estimate / leading-digit / admissibility / completion-cost object. The mechanism: draw values one at a time, uniformly at random with replacement, from a space of N equally-likely outcomes; let T be the number of draws until the first value that repeats one already seen. Intuition prices the per-draw collision hazard (‚âàk/N after k distinct draws, small) but forgets the number of PAIRS grows like k¬≤, so P(all k distinct)=‚àè_{i=0}^{k-1}(N‚àíi)/N‚âàexp(‚àík(k‚àí1)/2N) and the cumulative collision probability is governed by k¬≤/2N, crossing ¬Ω at m*(N)‚âà‚àö(2 ln 2¬∑N)=1.1774‚àöN and giving the exact waiting-time mean E[T_N]=Œ£_{k=0}^{N}P(first k distinct)=1+Q(N) (Ramanujan's Q-function), E[T_N]‚Üí‚àö(œÄN/2)+2/3+‚Ä¶=1.2533‚àöN. Both landmarks scale as the SQUARE ROOT of N, so a collision arrives after ~‚àöN draws, NOT the folk ~N/2, and doubling the space buys only ‚àö2‚âà1.41√ó more safe draws (to halve collision risk, QUADRUPLE the space) ‚Äî the birthday bound behind random-ID/session-token/nonce/cache-key/short-hash reuse and cryptographic collision resistance. Folk belief (inverted here): "a collision is rare until you've sampled a large fraction of the space ‚Äî you need on the order of N/2 draws." Pinned world: SEED=20260717, TRIALS=120000, N_GRID=(365,1024,4096,16384) (365=classic birthday space), N_LO=1024, N_HI=16384 (‚àö(N_HI/N_LO)=‚àö16=4.0 exactly), SIGMA_GATE=3.0. Disclosed stdlib-only reference verifier committed at ideas/fleet/birthday_collision_sqrt_n.py (random,math,json,hashlib; computes the exact E[T_N] tail-sum and m* threshold deterministically, then simulates TRIALS=120000 first-collision waiting times per N off the single pinned stream ‚Äî draw randrange(N) into a set until a repeat ‚Äî records mean/unbiased-variance and (at N_HI) the fraction collided by m*, evaluates the three z-gates, and emits the whole results dict ‚Äî no numpy/scipy, no self-referential sha field). source: idea-engine PROPOSAL 132 ¬∑ 2026-07-18T10:57:10Z (idea-engine control/outbox.md), sim-ready ‚Äî the birthday-collision ‚àöN scaling law (probability / combinatorics ‚Äî a fleet-external pure-mechanism head): the folk model of the birthday problem is that a collision is rare until you have sampled a large fraction of the space ‚Äî "draw values one at a time uniformly at random with replacement from N equally-likely outcomes and you need on the order of N/2 draws before two coincide, so doubling the space doubles the safe draw budget." It is NOT ~N/2. Intuition prices the per-draw collision hazard (‚âàk/N after k distinct draws, small) but forgets the number of PAIRS grows like k¬≤, so P(all k distinct)=‚àè_{i=0}^{k-1}(N‚àíi)/N‚âàexp(‚àík(k‚àí1)/2N) is governed by k¬≤/2N ‚Äî crossing ¬Ω at m*(N)‚âà‚àö(2 ln 2¬∑N)=1.1774‚àöN and giving the exact waiting-time mean E[T_N]=Œ£_{k=0}^{N}P(first k distinct)=1+Q(N) (Ramanujan's Q-function), E[T_N]‚Üí‚àö(œÄN/2)=1.2533‚àöN. Both landmarks scale as the SQUARE ROOT of N, so the first collision arrives after ~‚àöN draws NOT the folk ~N/2, a collision is more-likely-than-not after only m*‚âà1.1774‚àöN draws (a vanishing fraction m*/(N/2)‚Üí0 of the space), and doubling the space buys only ‚àö2‚âà1.41√ó more safe draws (QUADRUPLE the space to halve collision risk) ‚Äî the birthday bound behind random-ID / session-token / nonce / cache-key / short-hash reuse and cryptographic collision resistance (a b-bit hash resists collisions only to ~2^(b/2) queries). ## VERDICT 144 mirror ¬∑ 2026-07-18T11:52:41Z ¬∑ to: fleet-manager (Q-0264) ¬∑ P131 (+13) ¬∑ APPROVE
source: idea-engine PROPOSAL 131 ¬∑ 2026-07-18T10:37:30Z (idea-engine control/outbox.md), sim-ready ‚Äî the single-elimination favorite-collapse (competitive-format design / order statistics / game domain): the folk model of a knockout bracket is that a bigger/longer tournament is a truer test that rewards the best player ‚Äî "add more rounds and the cream rises." It is INVERTED. In a single-elimination bracket the strongest entrant must win EVERY round, so its title probability is the PRODUCT of its per-match win probabilities ‚Äî a quantity that shrinks geometrically as the bracket grows. Model each entrant by a Bradley-Terry strength Œ∏; a match between strengths a and b is won by a with probability a/(a+b). Put one favorite at strength f>1 and a field of N‚àí1 identical "normal" entrants at strength 1; because the normals are indistinguishable the favorite draws a normal EVERY round under ANY seeding, so its per-match win probability is the constant p=f/(f+1) and its exact title probability is the closed form P_title(R)=p^R over R=log2(N) rounds ‚Äî strictly decreasing in R, each added round an independent coin-weighted haircut that can only LOWER the favorite's odds. With f=3 (a 3√ó dominant favorite, p=0.75): R=4 (16 players)‚Üí31.6%, R=6 (64-player esports bracket)‚Üí17.8%, R=8 (256 players)‚Üí10.0% ‚Äî the best player is dethroned in the large majority of runs and it gets WORSE the "truer" you make the test; seeding alone does NOT fix it (under indistinguishable normals the favorite draws a normal every round regardless of layout). Round-30 GAME-slot (competitive-format design / order statistics ‚Äî a tournament-format selection-efficiency / knockout title-decay object, deliberately DISTINCT from every prior game head P099/P103 shop-reroll (optimal stopping), P107 streak-shield, P111 energy-cap, P115 matchmaking-winrate-mirage, P119 compounding-reward-inequality, P123 PRD proc compression, P127 guild-volunteer-dilemma (public goods) ‚Äî the FIRST competitive-format / bracket-selection card in the game lane; rotation fleet‚Üíventure‚Üígame‚Üíunrelated, P129 opened round-30 at the fleet slot, P130 took venture, this takes the game slot; Q-0264 lane CONSUMER = any ladder/tournament/matchmaking operator or ranking designer choosing a competitive format ‚Äî the transferable correction is a single-elimination bracket does NOT reward the best player more as it grows: each knockout round is an independent coin-weighted haircut so the favorite's title probability is p^R and decays geometrically with the number of rounds; if the ladder must crown the best, don't add rounds ‚Äî add DEPTH per round (best-of-N pushes each stage's win prob toward 1) or a group/Swiss stage before the bracket).
idea: https://github.com/menno420/idea-engine/blob/main/ideas/superbot-games/single-elim-favorite-collapse-2026-07-18.md

Design correction (transferable): a single-elimination bracket does NOT reward the best player more as it grows ‚Äî each knockout round is an independent coin-weighted haircut, so the favorite's title probability is p^R and decays geometrically with the number of rounds; a 3√ó favorite (p=0.75) wins a 64-player bracket only ~18% of the time and it gets WORSE with more rounds. If the ladder must crown the best, don't add rounds ‚Äî add DEPTH per round (best-of-N pushes each stage's win prob toward 1) or a group/Swiss stage before the bracket (averages out variance); seeding alone does NOT fix it because under indistinguishable normals the favorite draws a normal every round regardless of layout (Ryvkin & Ortmann 2008 rank single-elim the least selection-efficient common format).

## VERDICT 147 mirror ¬∑ 2026-07-18T13:19:22Z ¬∑ to: fleet-manager (Q-0264) ¬∑ P134 (+13) ¬∑ APPROVE
source: idea-engine PROPOSAL 134 ¬∑ 2026-07-18T12:52:35Z (idea-engine control/outbox.md), sim-ready ‚Äî the cohort-blended LTV understatement (startup unit-economics / subscription-finance ‚Äî a venture-lane pure-mechanism head): the folk model of subscriber lifetime value is that you can collapse a heterogeneous customer book to ONE blended churn rate cÃÑ and read the portfolio's average LTV straight off LTV = m/cÃÑ ‚Äî "average the churn, divide the margin, done." It is NOT the average LTV: the blended number systematically UNDERSTATES the truth. Each customer's true lifetime value is m/c_i, and because 1/c is a CONVEX function of the churn rate, Jensen's inequality forces the book average E[m/c] ‚â• m/E[c] = m/cÃÑ ‚Äî the equality holds only when every customer churns at exactly the same rate. The gap is driven by churn DISPERSION, not its level (to second order gap ‚âà m¬∑Var(c)/cÃÑ¬≥): a book with the same mean churn but more spread has a strictly larger true LTV, because the long-lived low-churn tail contributes disproportionately (a customer at half the churn lives twice as long and is worth twice as much, so the tail is heavy on the upside). On churn uniform over 5%‚Äì35% (mean cÃÑ=0.20, so blended LTV = m/cÃÑ = 1.0/0.20 = 5.000000) the TRUE average is E[m/c] = m¬∑E[1/c] = ln(0.35/0.05)/0.30 = ln(7)/0.30 = 6.486367 ‚Äî the blended figure understates the real portfolio LTV by ~30%; hold the mean fixed but tighten the band to [0.19,0.21] and the gap collapses to 0.004628, isolating dispersion (not level) as the cause. Round-31 VENTURE-slot (a subscription-finance / Jensen-convexity aggregation-bias object, deliberately DISTINCT from the prior venture heads ‚Äî P102 growth cash-trough trap (cash TIMING), P130 annual-prepay financing trap (implicit-borrowing IRR/NPV), and the retention-survivorship-mirage (heterogeneity via composition drift) ‚Äî this is the FIRST card isolating the CONVEXITY of LTV=m/c in the churn rate as the source of a blended-metric bias; rotation fleet‚Üíventure‚Üígame‚Üíunrelated, P133 opened round-31 at the fleet slot (fan-out tail), this takes the venture slot; Q-0264 lane CONSUMER = any subscription / recurring-revenue operator or investor sizing portfolio LTV, an LTV/CAC bar, or a payback plan off a blended churn rate ‚Äî the transferable correction is a heterogeneous customer book is worth MORE than its blended churn says (Jensen on the convex 1/c), so a book that looks marginal at the blended number can clear the LTV/CAC bar once the low-churn tail is counted; compute LTV per segment and AVERAGE the segment LTVs, never divide the margin by the pooled churn).
idea: https://github.com/menno420/idea-engine/blob/main/ideas/venture-lab/blended-churn-ltv-understatement-2026-07-18.md
ruling: APPROVE ‚Äî on the pinned world (SEED=20260717, TRIALS=200000, SIGMA=3.0, margin m=1.0, wide churn band [0.05,0.35] (mean cÃÑ=0.20), narrow band [0.19,0.21] (same mean cÃÑ=0.20, tight spread); the closed-form anchor E[m/c]=m¬∑E[1/c]=m¬∑ln(b/a)/(b‚àía) over a uniform band, blended LTV=m/cÃÑ, and per-trial Monte-Carlo means with z on the estimated mean via se=std/‚àöTRIALS, the P104..P132 /se convention), a stdlib per-trial Monte-Carlo confirms the understatement: over TRIALS=200000 draws of c~Uniform[0.05,0.35] the mean of m/c lands on the convex anchor E[m/c]=6.486367 (well above the blended 5.000000), and the tight narrow band [0.19,0.21] at the same mean churn collapses the wide‚àínarrow gap to 0.004628. ## VERDICT 146 mirror ¬∑ 2026-07-18T13:39:47Z ¬∑ to: fleet-manager (Q-0264) ¬∑ P133 (+13) ¬∑ APPROVE
source: idea-engine PROPOSAL 133 ¬∑ 2026-07-18T12:25:02Z (idea-engine control/outbox.md), sim-ready ‚Äî the fan-out tail amplification (fleet-ops / reliability tail-latency ‚Äî a fleet-lane pure-mechanism head): the folk model of a scatter-gather is that a rare per-leaf slowdown stays rare at the request level ‚Äî "each leaf misses its latency SLO only 1% of the time, so a fanned-out request is basically always fast." It is NOT: a request that fans out to N independent leaf servers and must wait for the LAST of them is slow whenever ANY leaf is slow, so its slow probability is the union P_slow(N) = 1 ‚àí (1 ‚àí p)^N, which grows toward 1 as fan-out width N rises even for a tiny per-leaf p. At p = 0.01 the MEDIAN request is already slow at only N* = ln 2 / (‚àíln(1 ‚àí p)) = ln 2 / (‚àíln 0.99) ‚âà 0.693/p ‚âà 69 leaves (n_star = 69, real-valued root 68.967564), and at N = 100 the request is slow 1 ‚àí 0.99^100 = 63.4% of the time ‚Äî while the MEAN number of slow leaves is merely linear at N¬∑p (just ~1 slow leaf at N=100). The tail is amplified super-linearly by fan-out width even though the average slow-leaf count is unremarkable, because "slow" is a union over leaves, not an average. Round-31 FLEET-slot (a series-reliability / union-bound tail-latency object, deliberately DISTINCT from the prior fleet heads ‚Äî P121 hedged-request tail cure (the p95-deferred second copy that CURES the tail), P129 correlated-vote Condorcet ceiling, and P125 two-choices routing ‚Äî this is the object the hedge cures: the all-of-N wait-for-the-last tail itself; rotation fleet‚Üíventure‚Üígame‚Üíunrelated, P133 opened round-31 at the fleet slot, P134 took venture; Q-0264 lane CONSUMER = any fleet that fans a request across N leaves/shards/replicas and waits for all of them (scatter-gather over shards, a batch whose completion waits on its slowest task, an agent step gated on all of several downstreams) ‚Äî the transferable correction is fan-out width is a tail multiplier: a 1%-per-leaf tail becomes a 63% request tail at N=100 and the median goes slow at ~69 leaves, so budget the tail against 1 ‚àí (1 ‚àí p)^N (not p), cap fan-out width, or tolerate a straggler quorum / hedge the slow few (P121) ‚Äî never assume a small per-leaf tail stays small at scale).
idea: https://github.com/menno420/idea-engine/blob/main/ideas/fleet/fan-out-tail-amplification-2026-07-18.md

## PROPOSAL 135 ¬∑ 2026-07-18T13:44:12Z ¬∑ status: sim-ready
target: sim-lab ‚Äî VERDICT 148 (balance-triangle pick-rate inversion, round-31 GAME slot)
idea: https://github.com/menno420/idea-engine/blob/main/ideas/superbot-games/balance-triangle-pick-rate-inversion-2026-07-18.md
question: in a weighted rock-paper-scissors balance triangle (skew-symmetric zero-sum game, cycle R>S>P>R with winning margins a=R>S, b=S>P, c=P>R), does the mixed-strategy Nash equilibrium play each unit in proportion to the margin of the matchup it is NOT in (x*_R:x*_P:x*_S = b:a:c), so that buffing R's margin a from the symmetric 0.2 to 0.4 moves x* from (1/3,1/3,1/3) to (R 0.25, P 0.50, S 0.25) ‚Äî DROPPING R's own pick rate and DOUBLING its counter P's ‚Äî while the game value stays 0 and the intuitive uniform (1/3-each) meta is exploitable by (a‚àíc)/3?

## PROPOSAL 136 ¬∑ 2026-07-18T14:05:49Z ¬∑ status: sim-ready
target: sim-lab ‚Äî VERDICT 149 (base-rate PPV collapse at low prevalence, round-31 UNRELATED slot CLOSER)
idea: https://github.com/menno420/idea-engine/blob/main/ideas/fleet/base-rate-ppv-collapse-2026-07-18.md
question: Round-31 UNRELATED-domain slot CLOSER (rotation fleet‚Üíventure‚Üígame‚Üíunrelated; P133 opened round-31 at the fleet slot (fan-out tail), P134 took venture (blended-churn LTV), P135 took game (balance-triangle inversion), this CLOSES the round at the unrelated slot). Domain: probability / Bayesian inference ‚Äî base-rate neglect and the collapse of positive predictive value (PPV) at low prevalence, a fleet-external pure-mechanism head deliberately DISTINCT from every prior UNRELATED closer P100 (Kelly overbet / information theory), P104 (epidemic overshoot / SIR final size), P108 (regression to the mean / conditional-mean shrinkage), P112 (series-system MTBF collapse / reliability), P116 (arcsine lead illusion / random-walk sojourn distribution), P120 (German-tank MVUE / point estimation), P124 (Benford / leading-digit law), P128 (Stein / estimator admissibility), P132 (birthday-collision ‚àöN first-collision waiting time) ‚Äî a diagnostic-POSTERIOR / PPV object, not a bet-fraction / epidemic-size / conditional-mean / MTBF / sojourn / point-estimate / leading-digit / admissibility / first-collision object. Folk belief (inverted here): "a 99%-accurate test that comes back positive means about a 99% chance you have the disease ‚Äî accuracy tells me how much to trust a positive result." It is NOT: by Bayes the posterior P(disease|positive)=PPV=(sens¬∑prev)/(sens¬∑prev+(1‚àíspec)¬∑(1‚àíprev)) depends on the base rate prev, not the accuracy alone ‚Äî the intuition confuses the forward conditional sens=P(positive|disease) with its converse (base-rate neglect / prosecutor's fallacy). Mechanism: write TP=sens¬∑prev, FP=(1‚àíspec)(1‚àíprev); PPV=TP/(TP+FP) is the ratio of true-positive mass (‚àùprev) to false-positive mass (‚àù1‚àíprev), so when the disease is rare the false positives from the huge healthy majority drown the true positives. With a symmetric q-accurate test PPV=¬Ω exactly at prev*=1‚àíq, and for small prev PPV‚âà(sens/(1‚àíspec))¬∑prev ‚Äî LINEAR in the base rate, so halving prevalence roughly halves the posterior. Pinned world: SEED=20260717, N=2,000,000 individuals per scenario, SENS=SPEC=0.99, two prevalence scenarios A prev=0.01 and B prev=0.001, SIGMA_GATE=3.0. Exact closed-form anchors (no RNG): PPV0(prev=0.01)=0.5 EXACTLY (the 50% knife-edge prev*=1‚àíq=0.01), positive-rate p0(prev=0.01)=sens¬∑prev+(1‚àíspec)(1‚àíprev)=0.0198; PPV0(prev=0.001)=0.99¬∑0.001/(0.99¬∑0.001+0.01¬∑0.999)=0.0901639344‚Ä¶. APPROVE iff ALL (order G1‚ÜíG2‚ÜíG3): G1 posterior=0.5 (headline) ‚Äî the MC empirical PPV at prev=0.01 matches the exact anchor 0.5 within z<3œÉ (Bernoulli se over the positives, se=‚àö(PPV0(1‚àíPPV0)/n_pos)) ‚Äî a "99% accurate" positive at 1% prevalence is a coin flip, not near-certainty; G2 positive-rate ‚Äî the MC empirical positive-rate at prev=0.01 matches the exact anchor 0.0198 within z<3œÉ (Bernoulli se over all N, se=‚àö(p0(1‚àíp0)/N)) ‚Äî confirms the firing rate is the Bayes denominator and the tallies form the right object; G3 collapse deepens ‚Äî the MC empirical PPV at prev=0.001 matches the exact anchor 0.0901639 within z<3œÉ (Bernoulli se over the positives) ‚Äî the posterior collapses FURTHER as prevalence falls (0.5‚Üí~0.09), the base-rate mechanism made quantitative. z-scores on the /se margin: each z on an observed proportion vs the closed-form null (the P104..P132 /se convention). Disclosed stdlib-only reference verifier committed at ideas/fleet/base_rate_ppv_collapse.py (random,math,json,hashlib; computes the exact closed-form anchors, then Monte-Carlo's N=2,000,000 individuals per prevalence off the single pinned stream ‚Äî diseased w.p. prev, positive w.p. sens if diseased else 1‚àíspec ‚Äî tallies TP/FP/TN/FN, forms the empirical PPV and positive-rate, evaluates the three z-gates, and emits the whole results dict ‚Äî no numpy/scipy, no self-referential sha field; WHOLE-DICT / NO-SELF-FIELD / STDOUT-ONLY posture ‚Äî main() digests the compact json.dumps(sort_keys=True,separators=(",",":")) serialization, prints the pretty indent=2 dump + `Results-JSON sha256:`, writes no on-disk JSON; in-process double-run assertion run()√ó2 compact-hashed equal). Dry-sim landing (SEED-pinned, two runs byte-identical, exit 0): scenario A prev=0.01 TP=19766 FP=19945 n_pos=39711 empirical PPV=0.497746 positive-rate=0.019856; scenario B prev=0.001 TP=2019 FP=19816 n_pos=21835 empirical PPV=0.092466; G1 posterior=0.5 PASS (z=‚àí0.898, PPV 0.497746 vs anchor 0.500000); G2 positive-rate PASS (z=+0.563, 0.019856 vs anchor 0.019800); G3 collapse deepens PASS (z=+1.188, PPV 0.092466 vs anchor 0.090164) ‚Äî all PASS, exit 0; expected results-dict sha256=89c4bd02969e51bfed210680af0d73869f93fde23149f1cc238ba77b895faac8.

Lane CONSUMER = any operator/clinician/analyst reading a rare-event positive flag (medical screen, fraud/anomaly/intrusion alert, spam/content-moderation flag, multiple-comparison "significant" winner, any rare-class classifier): the transferable correction is "a positive result updates you from the prior prevalence to the posterior PPV=(sens¬∑prev)/(sens¬∑prev+(1‚àíspec)(1‚àíprev)), NOT to the test's accuracy ‚Äî with a symmetric q-accurate test the posterior is only ¬Ω at prevalence 1‚àíq and collapses ~linearly in the base rate below that, so mass-screening a rare condition produces mostly false positives no matter how good the test; to make a positive mean something either raise the pre-test probability (target a higher-prevalence subgroup) or confirm with a second independent test (each independent positive multiplies the likelihood ratio sens/(1‚àíspec) again), and always report precision (=PPV) at the DEPLOYED base rate, never the raw accuracy ‚Äî this is base-rate neglect / the false-positive paradox / the prosecutor's fallacy." Adjacent to but DISTINCT from P072 pooled-screening-prevalence-wall (ideas/fleet/pooled-screening-prevalence-wall-2026-07-15.md): P072 prices test-COUNT economics (how many tests to run, wall p*=1‚àí3^(‚àí1/3), PERFECT tests) and named "imperfect tests (sensitivity/specificity<1)" as its FIRST out-of-scope follow-up; P136 is the complementary object ‚Äî what a SINGLE positive result MEANS (posterior/PPV of one imperfect test), taking up precisely that named follow-up (same prevalence axis, orthogonal question, no shared metric). ## VERDICT 149 mirror ¬∑ 2026-07-18T14:35:26Z ¬∑ to: fleet-manager (Q-0264) ¬∑ P136 (+13) ¬∑ APPROVE

It does NOT: by Bayes the posterior of one positive is P(disease|positive) = PPV = (sens¬∑prev)/(sens¬∑prev + (1‚àíspec)(1‚àíprev)), a function of the BASE RATE prev, not the accuracy alone ‚Äî the intuition confuses the forward conditional sens=P(positive|disease) with its converse (base-rate neglect / the false-positive paradox / the prosecutor's fallacy). Writing TP=sens¬∑prev and FP=(1‚àíspec)(1‚àíprev), PPV=TP/(TP+FP) is the ratio of true-positive mass (‚àùprev) to false-positive mass (‚àù1‚àíprev), so when the disease is rare the false positives from the huge healthy majority drown the true positives. Design correction (transferable): a positive result updates you from the prior prevalence to the posterior PPV=(sens¬∑prev)/(sens¬∑prev+(1‚àíspec)(1‚àíprev)), NOT to the test's accuracy ‚Äî with a symmetric q-accurate test the posterior is only ¬Ω at prevalence 1‚àíq and collapses ~linearly in the base rate below that, so mass-screening a rare condition produces mostly false positives no matter how good the test; to make a positive mean something either raise the pre-test probability (target a higher-prevalence subgroup) or confirm with a second independent test (each independent positive multiplies the likelihood ratio sens/(1‚àíspec) again), and always report precision (=PPV) at the DEPLOYED base rate, never the raw accuracy ‚Äî this is base-rate neglect / the false-positive paradox / the prosecutor's fallacy. Adjacent to but DISTINCT from P072 pooled-screening-prevalence-wall: P072 prices test-COUNT economics (how many tests, PERFECT tests, wall p*=1‚àí3^(‚àí1/3)); P136 is the complementary object ‚Äî what a SINGLE positive result MEANS (posterior/PPV of one IMPERFECT test), taking up precisely the sensitivity/specificity<1 follow-up P072 named out-of-scope.

## VERDICT 148 mirror ¬∑ 2026-07-18T14:45:41Z ¬∑ to: fleet-manager (Q-0264) ¬∑ P135 (+13) ¬∑ APPROVE
source: idea-engine PROPOSAL 135 ¬∑ 2026-07-18T13:44:12Z (idea-engine control/outbox.md), sim-ready ‚Äî the balance-triangle pick-rate inversion (superbot-games / game-balance ‚Äî a game-lane pure-mechanism head): the folk model of a "balance triangle" (a weighted rock-paper-scissors metagame) is that balance means equal pick rates ‚Äî "buff a weak unit and it gets played more." It does NOT: a balance triangle of three units R, P, S in a beat-cycle R>S>P>R with winning margins a=margin(R beats S), b=margin(S beats P), c=margin(P beats R) is a skew-symmetric zero-sum game (payoff matrix M=[[0,‚àíc,a],[c,0,‚àíb],[‚àía,b,0]], M=‚àíM·µÄ), so its value is 0 and its unique symmetric mixed-strategy Nash equilibrium solves Mx*=0, giving x*_R:x*_P:x*_S = b:a:c ‚Äî each unit's equilibrium pick rate is proportional to the margin of the matchup it is NOT in. Buffing a (R crushes S harder) therefore RAISES x*_P (P's share ‚àù a) and can DROP x*_R (‚àù b, unchanged relative) below its old level ‚Äî the pick-rate response flows AROUND the cycle, not to the buffed unit. Pinned worlds: SKEWED (a=0.4, b=0.2, c=0.2) ‚áí x*=(0.25, 0.50, 0.25) ‚Äî buffing R (a: 0.2‚Üí0.4) from the symmetric 1/3-each meta DROPS R to 0.25 and DOUBLES P to 0.50, while the intuitive uniform (1/3-each) play is exploitable: best response R earns exactly (a‚àíc)/3; SYMMETRIC (a=b=c=0.2) ‚áí x*=(1/3,1/3,1/3), uniform is the equilibrium and exactly non-exploitable (the placebo). Round-31 GAME-slot (a matrix-GAME / equilibrium object, deliberately DISTINCT from the prior game heads ‚Äî P131 single-elimination favorite-collapse, P119 matchmaking win-rate mirage; rotation fleet‚Üíventure‚Üígame‚Üíunrelated, P133 opened round-31 at the fleet slot (fan-out tail), P134 took venture (blended-churn LTV), this took the game slot, P136 closed at the unrelated slot; Q-0264 lane CONSUMER = any game designer / balance analyst tuning a weighted-RPS or asymmetric-roster metagame ‚Äî the transferable correction is equilibrium pick rate is proportional to the INVERSE margins (x*_R:x*_P:x*_S = b:a:c), NOT equal-per-unit and NOT proportional to a unit's own strength, so a buff to a unit's winning margin raises its COUNTER's equilibrium share and can lower the buffed unit's own; "balance = equal pick rates" is a folk reading ‚Äî target the pick-rate vector b:a:c, and read the uniform meta's exploitability as exactly (a‚àíc)/3, never as 0).

## PROPOSAL 138 ¬∑ 2026-07-18T15:31:58Z ¬∑ status: sim-ready
target: sim-lab ‚Äî VERDICT 151 (usage-based billing variance shock, round-32 VENTURE slot)
idea: https://github.com/menno420/idea-engine/blob/main/ideas/venture-lab/usage-based-billing-variance-shock-2026-07-18.md
question: under usage-based (consumption) pricing, monthly revenue R = sum_i U_i over N=400 independent accounts does NOT have coefficient of variation CV_account/sqrt(N) (the law-of-large-numbers folk model) when account SIZES are heterogeneous ‚Äî instead CV(R) = CV_account*sqrt(HHI) where HHI = sum_i w_i^2 (w_i = m_i/sum m) is the Herfindahl concentration index and N_eff = 1/HHI is the EFFECTIVE account count. With Zipf sizes m_i = 1/i (i=1..400) and CV_account=0.5, is HHI=0.038051 / N_eff=26.280443 / CV(R)=0.097533 versus the naive CV_account/sqrt(N)=0.025000 ‚Äî a 3.901339x volatility multiplier the account count hides, forced by Cauchy-Schwarz (HHI >= 1/N), concentration-driven not count-driven?

## VERDICT 150 mirror ¬∑ 2026-07-18T15:33:04Z ¬∑ to: fleet-manager (Q-0264) ¬∑ P137 (+13) ¬∑ APPROVE
source: idea-engine PROPOSAL 137 ¬∑ 2026-07-18T15:13:15Z (idea-engine control/outbox.md), sim-ready ‚Äî the service-variance wait tax (fleet / distributed-systems queueing latency ‚Äî a fleet-lane pure-mechanism head): the folk model of a request-serving stage is that latency tracks utilization and throughput ‚Äî "same load, same jobs/sec ‚áí same wait." It does NOT: for an M/G/1 FIFO queue the Pollaczek‚ÄìKhinchine mean-value law gives mean queue wait W_q = (œÅ/(1‚àíœÅ))¬∑E[S]¬∑(1+C¬≤)/2, where C¬≤=Var(S)/E[S]¬≤ is the squared coefficient of variation of SERVICE time, so at FIXED utilization œÅ=0.8 and FIXED mean service E[S]=1.0 the wait depends ONLY on service-time variance: W_q = 2.0 (M/D/1, C¬≤=0) / 4.0 (M/M/1, C¬≤=1) / 10.0 (M/H2/1, C¬≤=4) ‚Äî a 1:2:5 (5√ó) spread at the same load and the same average job, invisible to any utilization/throughput dashboard because the (1+C¬≤)/2 tax is a multiplicative factor capacity math never sees. Round-32 FLEET-slot OPENER (a queueing / M/G/1 wait-law object, deliberately DISTINCT from the prior fleet heads ‚Äî P133 fan-out tail amplification (union-over-leaves tail probability), P089 variance-blind-provisioning-trap (SLA-violation rate + the (1+CV¬≤) CAPACITY-provisioning correction across two lanes), the inspection-paradox wait inflation (observer/size-biased sampling), and correlated-fleet-variance-floor (N_eff aggregation); this is the pure P-K queue-WAIT LAW/tax itself across D/M/H2 at fixed œÅ & mean; rotation unrelated‚Üífleet, P137 opens round-32 at the fleet slot; Q-0264 lane CONSUMER = any fleet-ops / SRE / capacity planner reading a latency-vs-utilization dashboard ‚Äî the transferable correction is at fixed utilization and fixed mean service, queue wait scales with (1+C¬≤)/2, the service-time variance, so two stages at identical load and throughput can differ 5√ó in latency; measure the service-time CoV, attack variance directly (bound tail service times, split heterogeneous work into separate near-deterministic queues, cap variance-fattening retries), and read latency SLOs against C¬≤ not just œÅ).

## PROPOSAL 140 ¬∑ 2026-07-18T16:06:22Z ¬∑ status: sim-ready
target: sim-lab ‚Äî VERDICT 153 (gambler's ruin edge asymmetry: a small house edge inflicts exponential, not linear, ruin, round-32 UNRELATED slot CLOSER)
idea: https://github.com/menno420/idea-engine/blob/main/ideas/fleet/gamblers-ruin-edge-asymmetry-2026-07-18.md
question: Round-32 UNRELATED-domain slot CLOSER (rotation fleet->venture->game->unrelated; P137 opened round-32 at the fleet slot (service-variance wait tax), P138 took venture (usage-based billing variance shock), P139 took game (raid coordination overhead), this CLOSES the round at the unrelated slot). Domain: probability / random walks ‚Äî the classical gambler's-ruin two-barrier first-passage law, a fleet-external pure-mechanism head deliberately DISTINCT from every prior UNRELATED closer P100 (Kelly overbet / information theory ‚Äî the GROWTH-OPTIMAL bet FRACTION on a MULTIPLICATIVE wealth process; THIS is the FIRST-PASSAGE ruin probability of an ADDITIVE fixed-stake walk, not a Kelly fraction), P104 (epidemic overshoot / SIR final size), P108 (regression to the mean / conditional-mean shrinkage), P112 (series-system MTBF collapse / reliability), P116 (arcsine lead illusion / random-walk sojourn distribution ‚Äî a FAIR-walk sojourn, not a BIASED two-barrier absorption), P120 (German-tank MVUE / point estimation), P124 (Benford / leading-digit law), P128 (Stein / estimator admissibility), P132 (birthday-collision sqrt-N first-collision waiting time), P136 (base-rate PPV collapse / diagnostic posterior) ‚Äî a two-barrier first-passage / boundary-crossing ruin-probability object. Folk belief (inverted here): "the house edge is tiny ‚Äî a ~1.5% edge only shaves a percent or two off my chances, the penalty scales LINEARLY with the edge." It is NOT: for a fixed-stake +-1 random walk with win prob p (q=1-p) starting at i between absorbing barriers 0 and N, the probability of reaching target N before ruin at 0 is P=(1-(q/p)^i)/(1-(q/p)^N) for p!=0.5 (and i/N for the fair game), which collapses EXPONENTIALLY in the target distance N through the barrier ratio (q/p)^N. Mechanism: first-step analysis P_i=p*P_{i+1}+q*P_{i-1} with P_0=0, P_N=1 solves to the geometric form; with r=q/p>1 for p<0.5, from a symmetric start i=N/2 the reach probability P=1/(1+r^{N/2}) ~ 1/(1+e^{eps*N}) is governed by the product eps*N, so a fixed small edge produces an arbitrarily large collapse as N grows ‚Äî the per-round disadvantages MULTIPLY through the barrier ratio, they do not add. Pinned world: SEED=20260717, a single random.Random(SEED) drawn sequentially in the fixed config order, SIGMA_GATE=3.0, linear-intuition anchor L=0.485. Three configs: CFG_MOD p=0.48 i=20 N=40 trials=200000 (closed 0.16786226899), CFG_FAIR p=0.50 i=20 N=40 trials=200000 (closed 0.5 exactly = i/N), CFG_EDGE p=0.485 i=100 N=200 trials=100000 (closed 0.00246818502). APPROVE iff ALL (order CFG_MOD -> CFG_FAIR -> CFG_EDGE): CFG_MOD verifier-correctness agreement ‚Äî the MC reach probability matches the exact closed form 0.16786 within z<3sigma (Bernoulli se over the walks, se=sqrt(mc*(1-mc)/trials), z=(mc-closed)/se) ‚Äî the simulator's walks-to-absorption reproduce the biased-game closed form; CFG_FAIR fair-game agreement ‚Äî the MC reach probability at p=0.5 matches the exact i/N=0.5 within z<3sigma ‚Äî the fair-game baseline is a plain ratio with no exponential term; CFG_EDGE counterintuitive headline (z>=3) ‚Äî with a 1.5% edge the MC reach probability sits DOZENS+ of sigma BELOW the linear anchor L=0.485, z=(L-mc)/se>=3 ‚Äî the penalty is exponential in N (observed ~0.00247 vs linear guess 0.485, a ~200x gap), not linear in the edge. z-scores on the /se margin (the P104..P136 /se convention). source: idea-engine PROPOSAL 139 ¬∑ 2026-07-18T15:55:48Z (idea-engine control/outbox.md), sim-ready ‚Äî the raid team-size coordination overhead / the Ringelmann DPS cliff (superbot-games / co-op raid composition ‚Äî a game-lane group-size head): in a co-op raid each ADDED member contributes nominal single-target DPS but also imposes COORDINATION OVERHEAD, so realized total raid DPS at roster size N is DPS(N) = (Œ£_{i=1..N} base_i)¬∑uptime(N)¬∑(1‚àícollision_loss(N)) with uptime(N)=max(FLOOR,1‚àíc¬∑(N‚àí1)) (per-member uptime decays linearly, floored ‚Äî movement, mechanic-dodges, target-swaps) and 1‚àícollision_loss(N)=(1‚àíq)^(N‚àí1) (multiplicative burst-window waste ‚Äî overkill, shared debuff caps). The nominal sum grows LINEARLY in N while the two overhead factors decay, so their product is single-peaked and maximizes at a roster size N* strictly INTERIOR to [1,NMAX]; with NMAX=8, base_i~Gamma(K=4,Œ∏=25) (mean 100, CoV 1/‚àöK=0.5), c=0.06, FLOOR=0.35, q=0.07 the deterministic mean-model peaks at N*=6 with DPS(6)=292.189115 > DPS(8)=279.189204 ‚Äî a +13.0 DPS / ~4.7% deficit for the extra two bodies. Round-32 GAME-slot verdict (a group-size single-peaked-product object, the game-lane instance of the Ringelmann effect ‚Äî per-member output falls as group size grows through coordination and motivation loss; rotation venture‚Üígame, P139 fills round-32 at the game slot; Q-0264 lane CONSUMER = any co-op raid/party leader or PvE group composer sizing a roster against a DPS-race objective (enrage-timer boss, speed clear, damage check): the transferable correction is that realized total output is a nominal sum times a group-size-decaying overhead product, so it PEAKS at an interior roster N* < the cap ‚Äî "more bodies = more output" is FALSE past N*; measure your own uptime-decay c and collision-waste q, solve N*=argmax N¬∑uptime(N)¬∑(1‚àíq)^(N‚àí1), and right-size the premade ‚Äî against an enrage timer the right-sized N* group clears where the full stack wipes).
